## The "v1/v2" that DOES exist in this codebase:
These are **internal distributed protocol versions**, NOT REST API versions:
- `ConnectProtocol.CONNECT_PROTOCOL_V0 = 0` (ConnectProtocol.java) - Kafka group protocol for worker coordination
- `IncrementalCooperativeConnectProtocol.CONNECT_PROTOCOL_V1 = 1` - incremental cooperative rebalancing
- `IncrementalCooperativeConnectProtocol.CONNECT_PROTOCOL_V2 = 2` - with session key support

These are binary Kafka group protocol messages exchanged between workers, completely separate from the REST API.
